<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可行性判定程序主要针对正态分布观测数据，处理伯努利数据时需通过批次均值近似正态，这需要大样本量造成浪费。因此需要一种直接处理伯努利观测数据且支持主观多阈值的高效方法。

Method: 提出直接基于伯努利分布观测的可行性判定程序，支持多主观阈值；并提出两种启发式方法：当大量系统可行时收紧阈值，或当无可行系统时放松阈值。

Result: 实验表明该方法在统计上有效，且优于现有针对正态分布观测的可行性判定程序；两种启发式阈值调整策略能高效地为系统提供可行性判定。

Conclusion: 直接利用伯努利观测数据能提高效率，结合主观约束和动态阈值调整使方法更具实用性和灵活性。

Abstract: We consider the problem of determining feasible systems from a finite set of simulated alternatives with respect to probability constraints, where the observations from stochastic simulations are Bernoulli distributed. Most statistically valid procedures for feasibility determination focus on constraints on the means of normally distributed observations. Although these procedures can be adapted to Bernoulli-distributed data by treating batch means as basic observations, achieving approximate normality often requires a large batch size, potentially leading to the unnecessary waste of observations in reaching a decision. This paper proposes a procedure that utilizes the Bernoulli-distributed observations directly to determine feasibility. In addition, we incorporate subjective constraints, allowing for multiple thresholds for each constraint. We demonstrate that our proposed procedure is statistically valid and that it outperforms an existing feasibility determination procedure for subjective constraints originally developed for normally distributed observations. Furthermore, we propose two heuristic feasibility check approaches for thresholds that are sequentially added by decision makers, allowing thresholds to be tightened when many systems are feasible or relaxed when no feasible system exists. We show by experiments that the proposed procedures can efficiently provide feasibility decisions to systems with respect to all thresholds considered.

</details>


### [353] [Learning to reoptimize: a GNN-aided fix-and-optimize approach and an application to the Lot Sizing problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27339)
*Mathieu Lerouge,Andrea Lodi,Enrico Malaguti,Michele Monaci,Filippo Focacci*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出一种学习驱动的重新优化框架，利用图神经网络（GNN）指导修复策略，在机器故障等干扰导致原MILP求解的NP难问题解不可行时，快速生成高质量新解，在有限时间内显著优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实际运营中，NP难的组合优化问题（如MILP建模）常因不可预测干扰导致原解不可行。重新优化需要极短计算时间，而简单修复启发式方法解质量低。为弥合这一差距，需要一种既能快速响应又能保证解质量的重新优化方法。

Method: 设计了一个fix-and-optimize策略，结合图神经网络（GNN）：将实例、原始解和干扰信息编码为特征图，训练GNN预测哪些二元变量需要修改。基于预测选择少量变量由MILP求解器重新优化，其余变量固定不变。

Result: 在大数据集上的数值实验表明，该方法能有效处理不同规模的问题，并在有限时间预算内显著优于基线方法，实现更大的成本降低。

Conclusion: 提出一种学习驱动的重新优化框架，成功应用于机器故障干扰下的批量生产问题（LSP），能够快速生成高质量可行解，验证了GNN在指导组合优化修复中的有效性。

Abstract: In many operational contexts, solutions to NP-hard combinatorial optimization problems, modeled by means of Mixed-Integer Linear Programming (MILP), may become infeasible due to unpredictable disruptions. Typically, reoptimizing by solving the MILP formulation on the perturbed instance is not possible as new solutions must be obtained in a very short computing time, while simple repairing heuristics may result in low-quality solutions. To bridge this gap, we propose a learning-to-reoptimize framework, and apply it to the Lot Sizing Problem (LSP) under machine breakdown disruptions. We design a fix-and-optimize strategy aided by a Graph Neural Network (GNN) that efficiently computes a new solution within the neighborhood of a repaired solution. By representing the instance, the original solution and the disruption as a feature graph, we train a GNN to predict the likelihood that specific binary variables require to be modified. These predictions guide the selection of a small subset of variables to be reoptimized by an MILP solver, while the other variables are hard-fixed. Numerical experiments on a large dataset demonstrate that our approach handles effectively different problem sizes, and that it significantly outperforms a baseline alternative approach, yielding larger cost reductions within the same limited time budget.

</details>


### [354] [Stochastic global optimization of continuous functions via random walks on Grassmannians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14151)
*Kartik Gupta,Stephen D. Miller,Pradeep Ravikumar,Ramarathnam Venkatesan*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于Grassmannian流形上随机游走的全局优化方法。该方法在每次迭代中随机采样低维子空间（k≪d），并在其上求解原问题的低维限制，从而单调改进当前迭代点。收敛性保证不依赖凸性、光滑性等常规条件，而是取决于受限极小值在子空间中的几何分布，并引入类似谱间隙的"间隙参数"控制收敛速率。此外，该方法具有"盲点鲁棒性"：极小且极深的损失凹陷对算法轨迹影响有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有全局优化方法多依赖凸性、光滑性、Lipschitz界或Polyak-Lojasiewicz条件等假设，这些条件在现实高维问题中往往难以满足。作者试图设计一种不依赖这些传统假设的全局优化方法，仅基于随机子空间采样和几何分布特性来保证收敛。

Method: 方法核心为随机游走于Grassmannian流形：每次迭代采样一个随机k维线性子空间（k≪d），将原d维优化问题限制到该子空间上得到低维子问题，使用任意黑箱优化器求解该子问题，并利用解更新当前迭代点（保证单调改进）。重复此过程直至收敛。

Result: 理论上建立了收敛性分析，证明了收敛速率由"间隙参数"（类比马尔可夫链的谱间隙）控制，该参数刻画了受限极小值在k维子空间上的几何分布。此外，证明了该方法的"盲点鲁棒性"：极小测度区域内存在的极端低值（深而窄的凹陷）因随机采样不易命中，对算法轨迹影响有限。

Conclusion: 该工作提出了一种新颖的、不依赖传统光滑/凸性假设的全局优化框架，将优化问题与随机游走和Grassmannian几何联系起来。理论分析揭示了收敛速度的本质取决于子空间采样中极小值的分布几何，而非目标函数的局部光滑性质。盲点鲁棒性表明该方法在应对病态损失景观时具有天然优势。

Abstract: We introduce a stochastic global optimization method based on random walks on Grassmannian manifolds. To minimize a continuous objective $\ell:\mathbb{R}^d\rightarrow\mathbb{R}$, the method repeatedly samples random $k$-dimensional linear subspaces (with $k\ll d$), solves the resulting low-dimensional restrictions of these problems to these subspaces using an arbitrary black-box optimizer, and updates the iterate (which monotonically improves upon the previous iterate). Unlike classical optimization analyses that rely on convexity, smoothness, Lipschitz bounds, or Polyak-Lojasiewicz-type conditions, our convergence guarantees depend only on the geometric distribution of restricted minima across the $k$-dimensional subspaces passing through a given point in $\mathbb{R}^d$. We identify a gap parameter -- an analogue of a spectral gap for random walks -- that controls the rate at which the iterates approach the global minimum value. Finally, we argue that the same analysis yields a blind-spot robustness property: sufficiently narrow, deep dips of the loss function (small-measure regions where $\ell$ spikes downward) have limited influence on the algorithm's trajectory, since they are unlikely to be encountered by random subspace sampling.

</details>

### [355] [Low Latency Stand Alone Compute-Efficient Forecasting of Marine Engine Time Series Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26123)
*Y. Harsha Vardhana Reddy,Soumyendu Raha*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于自适应窗口多粒子随机微分方程的鲁棒数学框架，用于高性能船舶发动机参数的非线性状态空间预测。该方法通过自适应回溯机制和多粒子集成，结合Girsanov变换概率测度调整，显著优于传统统计模型，适用于高波动性和非线性系统的实时风险量化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高性能船舶推进系统面临多样化运行载荷和环境应力，其运行可靠性高度依赖系统健康状态。传统时间序列模型（如VARIMA）因固定窗口线性假设，无法捕捉复杂系统的固有随机性和瞬态动力学特性，亟需更鲁棒的预测框架。

Method: 提出双层估计方法：1) 自适应回溯机制，根据瞬时漂移幅度动态调整学习窗口大小；2) 多粒子集成，通过Euler-Maruyama离散化演化各粒子轨迹，代表系统状态的不同随机实现；3) 引入Girsanov变换改变概率测度，对符合物理漂移的粒子赋予更高权重，抑制"追逐噪声"行为。

Result: 理论评估和实证基准测试表明，所提出的自适应SDE框架在多步预测稳定性和计算效率方面显著优于经典统计基线模型。

Conclusion: 该模型提供了一种可扩展的"灰箱"解决方案，适用于具有高频波动性和非线性过渡特征系统的实时风险量化，为船舶推进系统运行可靠性评估提供了有效工具。

Abstract: The operational reliability of a high performance marine vessel depends critically on the health of its marine propulsion systems, which are increasingly subjected to diverse operational loads and environmental stressors. This paper proposes a robust mathematical framework for non-linear state-space forecasting of marine engine parameters using adaptive-window multi-particle stochastic differential equations. Traditional time-series models such as Vector Autoregressive Integrated Moving Average, often fail to capture the inherent stochasticity and transient dynamics of complex systems due to their reliance on fixed-window linear assumptions. To address this, we develop a dual-layered estimation approach: first, an adaptive lookback mechanism dynamically adjusts the learning window size based on the instantaneous drift magnitude, ensuring responsiveness during non-stationary regimes. Second, a Multi-Particle ensemble is evolved via Euler-Maruyama discretization, where each particle trajectory represents a stochastic realization of the system state. To refine the ensemble mean and mitigate the "noise-chasing" behavior of raw estimators, a Girsanov transform induced change of probability measure is implemented, assigning higher probabilistic weights to particles that align with the physical drift. Theoretical evaluation and empirical benchmarking demonstrate that the proposed adaptive SDE framework significantly outperforms classical statistical baselines in multi-step prediction stability and computational efficiency. The model provides a scalable, "grey-box" solution for real-time risk quantification in systems characterized by high-frequency volatility and non-linear transitions.

</details>

Abstract: This paper proposes a systematic framework to assess the small-signal stability of power systems with high shares of grid-following inverter-based resources (IBRs) under varying controller parameters and operating conditions. Full-network linearization and eigenvalue analysis are combined with adaptive sampling based on probabilistic support vector machine classification to approximate stability boundaries efficiently, while surrogate optimization identifies feasible initial controller settings meeting bandwidth and phase-margin constraints. The approach is validated on a modified Cigré European HV network benchmark with 50 operating scenarios and increasing inverter penetration. Results show that stability sensitivity grows with inverter share, interactions among IBRs reshape admissible parameter regions, and simplified equivalent-network models may overlook critical system-level limitations. The framework supports stability-oriented controller design and interconnection studies in converter-dominated systems.

### [358] [Orion: Enabling Self-adaptive Memory Management for On-device Online Continual Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26473)
*Zexin Li,Nikil Dutt,Cong Liu*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: Orion是一个面向资源受限设备（如自主机器人）的在线持续学习（OCL）框架，通过统一运行时指标URGE（基于"木桶效应"原理）动态协调批处理、回放缓冲区和优化策略，协同优化训练延迟、可塑性与稳定性。系统原型在多种OCL算法、基准和硬件平台上验证，并在现实自主导航机器人中集成，实现了显著训练加速与均衡性能，开销极低。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在线持续学习（OCL）在资源受限系统上面临内存约束，影响训练延迟、可塑性和稳定性之间的关键权衡。离线参数调优无法适应OCL过程中动态变化的内存压力和工作负载复杂度，因此需要一种在线且自适应的方案来实现鲁棒的设备端部署。

Method: 提出Orion框架，核心是URGE（统一运行时指标），基于"木桶效应"原理（系统性能受最稀缺资源制约），在操作系统和应用层面联合协调批处理、回放缓冲区和优化策略，动态重新分配OCL组件间的内存。同时引入系统级数据预取技术以最大化效率。

Result: 基于Avalanche-lib实现系统原型，在多种OCL算法、基准和硬件平台上评估，并在现实自主导航机器人中集成。结果表明Orion实现显著训练加速，保持均衡性能，有效适应各种场景，且运行时、内存和能耗开销极小。

Conclusion: Orion是一种实用的设备端持续学习解决方案，通过在线自适应内存协调有效解决了资源受限下的OCL部署难题，在训练效率、可塑性与稳定性之间取得了良好平衡。

Abstract: Online continual learning (OCL) enables real-time adaptation to new data, making it crucial for dynamic robotic applications. However, its practical deployment is hindered by memory constraints in resource-limited systems, which affect key trade-offs in training latency, plasticity, and stability. Unlike offline parameter tuning, which cannot account for the dynamic shift in memory pressure and workload complexity as OCL progresses, an online and self-adaptive approach is essential for robust on-device deployment. This paper proposes Orion, a holistic framework designed to co-optimize training latency, plasticity, and stability of state-of-the-art OCL models under strict memory constraints, enabling feasible on-device deployment. At its core, Orion leverages URGE, a unified runtime indicator grounded in the ``Buckets effect'' principle that system performance is bounded by its scarcest resource, to dynamically reallocate memory across OCL components by jointly coordinating batch processing, replay buffers, and optimization strategies at both the OS and application level. Furthermore, Orion introduces system-level data prefetching techniques to maximize efficiency. A system prototype of Orion has been implemented using the widely adopted \texttt{Avalanche-lib} and thoroughly evaluated across a diverse range of OCL algorithms, benchmarks, and hardware platforms commonly used in autonomous robotic applications. To further demonstrate its practical utility, Orion is integrated into a realistic autonomous navigational robot powered by OCL. The results show that Orion achieves significant training speedups while maintaining balanced performance and effectively adapting to various scenarios, all with minimal runtime, memory, and energy overhead, making Orion a practical solution for on-device continual learning.

</details>

*Haoyu Li,Xiangru Zhong,Hao Cheng,Bin Hu,Huan Zhang*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文提出一个统一框架，将控制理论与先进的神经网络验证器α,β-CROWN结合，用于安全关键系统中控制器属性的形式化验证（如稳定性和安全性）。α,β-CROWN作为通用非线性函数边界计算引擎，通过计算紧致边界、递归划分子域并利用GPU并行化，实现了对高维神经网络系统可扩展的验证与优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 该框架在传统方法难以处理的验证和优化问题上展现出优越的可扩展性，得益于GPU并行化，能够处理高维神经网络系统。

Conclusion: 本文教程介绍了α,β-CROWN的基础知识及其在多种控制相关任务中的应用，弥合了控制理论与先进神经网络验证器之间的鸿沟，为安全关键场景下的控制器形式化验证提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Learning-based methods for synthesizing controllers have gained popularity due to their high expressiveness and strong empirical performance. However, in safety-critical scenarios such as autonomous driving, robotics, and power systems, empirical performance alone is insufficient, and formal verification of controller properties such as stability and safety is highly desirable. Unfortunately, many prior verification approaches are either tied to specific structural assumptions on the system or the certificate, making them difficult to transfer across settings, or suffer from poor scalability on higher-dimensional neural network systems. In this tutorial, we present a unified framework that aims to mitigate this gap via bridging control with the state-of-the-art neural network verifier $α,\!β$-CROWN (alpha-beta-CROWN). At its core, $α,\!β$-CROWN is a general-purpose bounding engine for nonlinear functions represented as computation graphs: given an input domain, it can produce certified bounds and explicit linear relaxation of the nonlinear function. These certified bounds are useful on their own for tasks such as reachability analysis, and they also provide the foundation for more complex routines that perform satisfiability checking and optimization. More specifically, many control problems reduce to verifying real-valued inequalities over a state domain (e.g., Lyapunov theory). Consequently, $α,\!β$-CROWN enables scalable verification of such conditions by computing tight bounds and recursively partitioning and pruning subdomains based on the bounds. Thanks to GPU parallelization, this pipeline demonstrates superior scalability on verification and optimization problems that are challenging for traditional approaches. In this tutorial, we discuss the basics of $α,\!β$-CROWN and introduce its application to various control-related tasks.

Abstract: Stochastic model-predictive control (SMPC) has evolved to a powerful framework for the control of stochastic dynamical systems. SMPC utilizes a probabilistic uncertainty description to provide a systematic trade-off between the control objective and constraint satisfaction in a statistical sense. However, the majority of existing SMPC methods face challenges related to computational tractability due to the need for stochastic inference. Approaches that apply accurate inference are computationally demanding, which can lead to serious limitations in the implementability of these methods. Hence, in practice, the uncertainty propagation and the resulting distributions are typically approximated, e.g., by Gaussian distributions. To overcome this fundamental limitation of SMPC approaches, we propose a novel formulation based on the meta-state-space (MSS) representation of stochastic dynamical systems. The proposed MSS-based SMPC scheme offers a computationally efficient way to forward propagate the uncertainty with a flexible and highly accurate approximation of the probabilistic system description. With the presented method, the entire output probability density function can be directly shaped, which is unprecedented among existing SMPC techniques. Finally, we provide a detailed theoretical analysis and demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed methodology via an extensive simulation study.

### [363] [Breaking the Epistemic Trap: Active Perception Under Compound Uncertainty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26627)
*Chayan Banerjee,Ethan Goan*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文指出强化学习在安全关键领域（如自动驾驶、医疗决策）失败的根本原因是“认知陷阱”——动态变化与观测不完整之间的协同作用，并提出了一个主动感知的安全架构（Adaptive Safety Architecture），包含复合不确定性系数κ、MaxInfoRL目标函数和自适应安全约束，以解决这种耦合不确定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习方法在面对动态变化和不完整观测时表现不佳，因为这两者协同作用（而非单独作用）会导致严重的性能退化（77% vs 46%）。作者认为当前方法采取被动认知立场，无法解决耦合不确定性，需要重新框架化安全问题为信息问题。

Method: 1) 提出Compound Uncertainty Coefficient (κ)，基于互信息的度量，可在线计算状态-动态耦合程度；2) 提出MaxInfoRL目标函数，驱动智能体主动探索系统动态；3) 设计自适应安全约束，随认知耦合程度增强而收紧。

Result: 概念验证实验显示，耦合不确定性导致77%的性能退化，而单独叠加仅46%，证明了协同失效模式的严重性。常规方法无法处理这种耦合不确定性。

Conclusion: 从被动鲁棒性转向主动感知，系统能在不确定性下运行、识别自身无知并通过信息寻求行为策略性地解决无知，为安全关键决策提供了原则性路径。

Abstract: Deploying reinforcement learning in safety critical domains, from autonomous vehicles to medical decision support, is constrained by failures arising when systems encounter unfamiliar conditions. We argue that the fundamental bottleneck is not individual challenges like changing dynamics or incomplete observations, but their synergistic interaction, which we term the Epistemic Trap: agents cannot estimate their state without knowing system dynamics, nor learn dynamics without accurate state information. Proof-of-concept experiments in simulated locomotion reveal that combining these uncertainties causes failures far worse than either challenge alone, a 77% performance degradation against the 46% by adding the individual effects, demonstrating compounding failure modes that conventional methods overlook. Such approaches adopt a passive epistemic stance that cannot resolve this coupled uncertainty. We propose reframing safety as an information problem, introducing an Adaptive Safety Architecture built around three contributions: the Compound Uncertainty Coefficient ($κ$), a mutual information based metric that quantifies state dynamics coupling and is computable online without full joint belief inference; information seeking policies governed by a MaxInfoRL objective that actively probe system dynamics; and regime-adaptive safety constraints that tighten as epistemic coupling rises. This paradigm shift, from passive robustness to active perception, offers a principled path toward decision making systems that operate under uncertainty, recognize their own ignorance, and act strategically to resolve it.

### [364] [Sample Complexity of Policy Gradient for Log-Growth Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.26640)
*Qiuhua Pan,Yukai Shen,Liwei Zhang,Cailian Chen,Xinping Guan*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文研究了用于对数增长控制的策略梯度样本复杂度问题，发现最优增益处存在“尖点障碍”（策略梯度仅以柯西主值存在，单样本估计器方差无穷大），并提出利用对称性配对观测样本消除发散部分，证明了投影小批量策略梯度在已知和未知噪声密度条件下的样本复杂度上界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准一阶随机优化分析在最优增益处失效（梯度不存在为Lebesgue积分，单样本估计器方差无穷大），需要新的理论工具来刻画此问题的样本复杂度。

Method: 利用柯西核是奇函数的对称性，将每个观测与其关于极点的反射配对，消除发散部分；结合闭式单跳变梯度预言，分析投影小批量策略梯度的收敛性。

Result: 噪声密度已知时样本复杂度为$\tilde{O}(1/η)$；需估计噪声密度（$C^s$类，$s \geq 2$）时为$\tilde{O}(η^{-(2s+1)/(2s)})$。

Conclusion: 通过对称性配对策略即可克服结构性的尖点障碍，实现有效的策略梯度学习。

Abstract: We study the sample complexity of policy gradient for log-growth control -- the problem of learning, from observed state transitions, a feedback gain that optimally stabilizes a scalar linear system driven through a multiplicative-noise actuation channel. The objective $J(K) = \mathbb{E}[\log|1+BK|]$ is the top Lyapunov exponent of the closed loop. This problem carries a structural difficulty we call the cusp obstruction: the optimal gain $K^*$ always places the noise singularity $b_{\rm sing}(K) = -1/K$ in the interior of the support. At this singular optimum the policy gradient exists only as a Cauchy principal value, not as a Lebesgue integral, and the natural single-sample gradient estimator has infinite variance. Standard first-order stochastic-optimization analysis is thus inapplicable at the optimum, and merely smoothing the objective does not resolve the difficulty. The obstruction, however, has an exploitable symmetry: the Cauchy kernel is an odd function of the displacement from the moving pole, so pairing each observation with its reflection through the pole cancels the divergent part. This one cancellation simultaneously controls the population curvature, the gradient-estimator variance, and the bias incurred when the noise density is estimated. Combining these bounds with a closed-form single-transition gradient oracle, we prove that projected mini-batch policy gradient, initialized in any compact subset of the stabilizing region, attains total sample complexity $\tilde{O}(1/η)$ when the noise density is known and $\tilde{O}(η^{-(2s+1)/(2s)})$ when it must be estimated, for $C^s$ noise densities with $s \geq 2$.

</details>

Then, we utilize an extended Kalman filter and pseudo-measurements in combination with a ReLU pseudo-measurement function to enforce soft inequality constraints. This work builds upon a previously published conference paper with the same goal and a similar fundamental approach. Opposite to our previous work, however, we now use an exact covariance calculation for the RGP gradients. Furthermore, we also present a real-time optimized version of this algorithm with less simplifications compared to the previously published version. These and several other algorithmic innovations lead to an algorithm with greatly improved numerical robustness. The algorithm is validated and compared to its previously published version for a 2D numerical example.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有反无人机蜂群防御方法未能同时处理攻击者时变交互结构、防御方感知不确定性以及切换分配带来的不稳定性问题。

Method: 1) 基于概率图的蜂群表示（从不确定观测中推断）；2) 风险感知的 attacker 临界性模型（结合时间紧迫度与不确定性）；3) 在线 defender 分配与选择性重分配机制（含鲁棒执行约束以抑制切换不稳定）；4) 基于过滤的首次命中时间理论分析框架。

Result: 概率感知下中和效率85.6%，确定性感知下99.9%；给出了期望中和时间的混合线性-几何上界；消融实验量化了检测阈值与协调参数的影响。

Conclusion: 所提出的不确定性感知闭环框架能有效应对蜂群入侵，理论保证与仿真结果一致，检测质量是影响效率的关键因素。

Abstract: This article presents a closed-loop, uncertainty-aware framework for defending a protected zone against coordinated incursions by swarms of small uncrewed aircraft systems (UAS). The interaction structure of the attackers is modeled as time-varying, while defenders operate under imperfect sensing. The proposed criticality-driven defender-to-attacker assignment strategy integrates three components: a probabilistic graph-based representation of the attacking swarm inferred from uncertain observations; a risk-aware attacker criticality model combining time-to-breach urgency with uncertainty; an online defender allocation mechanism that assigns and selectively reassigns defenders while limiting switching-induced instability through robust execution constraints. Analytical guarantees are established within a filtration-based first-hitting-time framework. In particular, finite-time triggering of the first capture event following detection is proven, and explicit mixed linear-geometric upper bounds are derived for the expected neutralization time. Monte Carlo simulations demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed framework, achieving 85.6% neutralization efficiency under probabilistic sensing and 99.9% under deterministic sensing. Systematic ablation and sensitivity studies further quantify how detection thresholds and coordination parameters influence reliability and time-to-first-capture.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有动态电价方法依赖详细的用户级消费数据和行为模型，难以获取且存在隐私问题；亟需一种仅需有限观测数据（如聚合负荷）就能有效削峰的电价设计方法。

Method: 提出在线反馈优化（OFO）算法，通过迭代更新日前电价，仅利用聚合负荷测量值进行优化，并加入对总用电成本偏差的惩罚项，无需个体用户数据。

Abstract: The growing adoption of electric vehicles (EVs) is increasing peak demand in distribution systems, which can threaten grid stability and reduce operational efficiency. Dynamic electricity pricing is a promising means of mitigating these peaks by shifting flexible demand. However, most existing approaches rely on detailed user-level consumption data and behavioral models, which are often difficult to obtain in practice and may raise privacy concerns.
  This paper proposes an Online Feedback Optimization (OFO) algorithm for day-ahead price design with limited data, where only aggregate loads are observed. OFO updates prices iteratively using aggregate load measurements, enabling effective peak reduction without access to individual user data. The formulation also includes a term that penalizes deviations in total electricity cost relative to a reference tariff. Although relying only on aggregate load measurements, the OFO price updates efficiently converge to the optimal price. In finite-horizon simulations, OFO achieves peak reduction close to that of the Stackelberg benchmark with full model information. Meanwhile, its computational effort is substantially lower. Additional tests under multiple initial conditions and delayed charging-window mismatch further confirm the robustness of the proposed method. Overall, these results show that OFO is a scalable and computationally efficient approach for peak-demand management in distribution systems with limited observability.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种基于图的建模方法，将暂态能量守恒定律与系统的网络拓扑结构显式结合，通过图结构表示能量的存储和传递关系。文中给出了数学模型概述，并提供了单相/两相热系统、机电系统等多域组件和系统模型的示例。

Abstract: Modern energy systems in vehicles and built infrastructure are governed by high-dimensional dynamics spanning multiple physical domains (e.g., electrical, thermal, mechanical) and timescales. This tutorial paper presents a graph-based modeling approach created to facilitate the modeling, analysis, control, estimation, optimization, and design of these systems. Matured and validated through more than a decade of research spanning multiple academic institutions and companies, the graph-based approach combines transient energy conservation with an explicit mathematical representation of the network by which energy is stored and transferred within a system. Following a mathematical overview of graph-based models, examples of multi-domain component and system models from the recent literature are presented, including single-phase thermal systems, two-phase thermal systems, and electro-mechanical systems. This is followed by a survey of recent applications for decentralized and hierarchical model predictive control, design optimization, and control co-design. Lastly, the paper describes an open-source toolbox created to facilitate the generation and analysis of graph-based models.

### [371] [In-Orbit Intelligence or Ground Offloading? Inference Freshness under Intermittent Satellite Connectivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27021)
*Ayse Nur Pehlivanoglu,Aimin Li,Elif Uysal*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文研究了在间歇性低轨卫星连接下，如何平衡星上计算与地面计算以优化推理新鲜度。通过定义“推理年龄”（AoInf）作为性能指标，并构建半马尔可夫决策过程模型，提出了混合策略，相比纯星上或纯卸载方案，在降低平均AoInf的同时节省了计算与通信资源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低轨卫星与地面站之间的连接具有间歇性特点，如何在有限的星上资源与地面资源之间合理分配推理任务，以保持推理结果的时效性（即"新鲜度"），是一个关键挑战。现有方法多为纯星上计算或纯数据卸载，未能有效权衡资源消耗与信息新鲜度。

Method: 定义了Age of Inference (AoInf)指标，将问题建模为有限状态平均成本半马尔可夫决策过程（SMDP），状态包括地面AoInf、轨道接触相位、缓存占用和缓存年龄。通过将SMDP转化为等效的平均成本MDP，并使用归一化相对值迭代（RVI）求解最优策略。

Result: 数值结果表明，所提出的混合策略相比纯星上计算和纯卸载基线，能够降低平均AoInf，同时相比纯星上计算节省了星上计算资源，相比纯卸载节省了通信资源。

Conclusion: 在间歇性LEO连接条件下，通过混合策略（星上计算、缓存语义传输、原始数据卸载、等待）动态切换，可以在资源受限场景下实现更优的推理新鲜度，兼顾计算与通信效率。

Abstract: This paper studies how to balance onboard and ground computation under intermittent LEO connectivity for optimized inference freshness. As connectivity varies in time, the system switches among the actions of onboard computation, cached semantic transmission, raw-data offloading, and waiting. We define Age of Inference (AoInf) as the performance metric, where the age resets only upon successful task-valid updates. We formulate long-run average AoInf minimization as a finite-state average-cost semi-Markov decision process whose state captures the ground AoInf, orbital contact phase, cache occupancy, and cache age. We then transform the SMDP into an equivalent average-cost MDP and compute the solution via normalized relative value iteration (RVI). Numerical results indicate that the resulting hybrid policy reduces average AoInf relative to onboard-only and offload-only baselines, while requiring less computational resources on the satellite than the former, and fewer communication resources than the latter.

</details>

The approach employs a mixed-integer formulation to optimize charging-related costs across charging, operation, battery degradation, and congestion delay, considering a range of scenarios. ### [373] [Container Unloading via Reinforcement Learning: Picking Order, Deadlock Avoidance, and Proof-of-Concept Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27143)
*Jan Rüdiger,Max Schenke,Daniel Weber*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建仿真环境，采用带掩码的深度Q学习（Masked Deep Q-Learning）结合特殊设计的神经网络架构，用于学习物品选择策略。

Abstract: Unloading containers in the courier, express and parcel industry is a physically demanding and labor-intensive work. This work investigates the potential of reinforcement learning to learn a policy for item selection in container unloading scenarios. For that, a simulation environment is created and a masked deep Q-learning with a specially designed neural network architecture is implemented. The results indicate that the agent can learn to select items with an average success rate of 60 %, which is significantly better than a random policy at a random chance of 20 %. The findings suggest that RL could be a promising approach for automatizing item unloading tasks in the future.
